## currency settler BaseHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";‚êä
    import {CurrencySettler} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/utils/CurrencySettler.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseHook {‚êä
        using CurrencySettler for Currency;‚êä
    ‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager) BaseHook(_poolManager) {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: false,‚êä
                afterInitialize: false,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: false,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä
                beforeDonate: false,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä
    `

## access control (ownable) BaseHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseHook, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: false,‚êä
                afterInitialize: false,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: false,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä
                beforeDonate: false,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä

                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä

## access control (roles) BaseHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseHook, AccessControl {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address defaultAdmin)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
        {‚êä
            _grantRole(DEFAULT_ADMIN_ROLE, defaultAdmin);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: false,‚êä
                afterInitialize: false,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: false,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä
                beforeDonate: false,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,‚êä

    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {AccessManaged} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/manager/AccessManaged.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseHook, AccessManaged {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialAuthority)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            AccessManaged(initialAuthority)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: false,‚êä
                afterInitialize: false,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä

                beforeSwap: false,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä

## pausable BaseHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseHook, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: false,‚êä
                afterInitialize: false,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä
    `

## inversed mixed permissions BaseAsyncSwap

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä

    ‚êä

    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Implement how asynchronous swaps are executed‚êä
    // i.e. queuing swaps to be executed together in batches, reordering, etc‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseAsyncSwap {‚êä

## access control (roles) BaseAsyncSwap

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä

    ‚êä
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseAsyncSwap} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseAsyncSwap.sol";‚êä

## pausable BaseAsyncSwap

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BaseAsyncSwap} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseAsyncSwap.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Implement how asynchronous swaps are executed‚êä
    // i.e. queuing swaps to be executed together in batches, reordering, etc‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseAsyncSwap, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: false,‚êä
                afterInitialize: false,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä
    `

## transient storage BaseCustomAccounting

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä

## pausable BaseCustomAccounting

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseCustomAccounting} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseCustomAccounting.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the accounting logic‚êä
    // i.e. liquidity mining, rewarding well-behaved LPs, etc‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseCustomAccounting, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getAddLiquidity(uint160 sqrtPriceX96, AddLiquidityParams memory params)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes memory, uint256)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how liquidity additions and minted shares are computed‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getRemoveLiquidity(RemoveLiquidityParams memory params)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes memory, uint256)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how liquidity removals and burned shares are computed‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _mint(AddLiquidityParams memory params, BalanceDelta callerDelta, BalanceDelta feesAccrued, uint256 shares)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how shares are minted‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _burn(RemoveLiquidityParams memory params, BalanceDelta callerDelta, BalanceDelta feesAccrued, uint256 shares)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how shares are burned‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function addLiquidity(AddLiquidityParams calldata params)‚êä
            public‚êä
            payable‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (BalanceDelta)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super.addLiquidity(params);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function removeLiquidity(RemoveLiquidityParams calldata params)‚êä
            public‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (BalanceDelta)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super.removeLiquidity(params);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä
                afterInitialize: false,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä

## pausable BaseCustomCurve

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseCustomCurve} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseCustomCurve.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä

    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the pricing curve‚êä
    // i.e. specialized pricing curves, etc‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseCustomCurve, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getUnspecifiedAmount(SwapParams calldata params)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (uint256)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the unspecified currency amount is computed‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getSwapFeeAmount(SwapParams calldata params, uint256 unspecifiedAmount)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (uint256)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the LPs fees amount is computed‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getAmountOut(RemoveLiquidityParams memory params)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (uint256, uint256, uint256)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the amount out of the swap is computed‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getAmountIn(AddLiquidityParams memory params)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (uint256, uint256, uint256)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the amount in of the swap is computed‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _mint(AddLiquidityParams memory params, BalanceDelta callerDelta, BalanceDelta feesAccrued, uint256 shares)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how shares are minted‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _burn(RemoveLiquidityParams memory params, BalanceDelta callerDelta, BalanceDelta feesAccrued, uint256 shares)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how shares are burned‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function addLiquidity(AddLiquidityParams calldata params)‚êä
            public‚êä
            payable‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (BalanceDelta)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super.addLiquidity(params);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function removeLiquidity(RemoveLiquidityParams calldata params)‚êä
            public‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (BalanceDelta)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super.removeLiquidity(params);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä
                afterInitialize: false,‚êä

            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap‚êä
        }‚êä

                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä

## access control (roles) BaseDynamicFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseDynamicFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseDynamicFee.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä

        }‚êä
    ‚êä

            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity‚êä

## pausable BaseDynamicFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BaseDynamicFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseDynamicFee.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the LP fee for the entire pool‚êä
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, etc‚êä
    contract MyHook is Ownable, BaseDynamicFee, ERC20, Pausable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getFee(PoolKey calldata key) internal override returns (uint24) {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the LP fee is computed‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function poke(PoolKey calldata key) public onlyOwner whenNotPaused {‚êä
            _poke(key);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä
                afterInitialize: true,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä

## pausable BaseOverrideFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseOverrideFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseOverrideFee.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap‚êä
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the LP fee is computed‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä
                afterInitialize: true,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: false,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä

    ‚êä

    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä

        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä

            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity‚êä
        }‚êä

        function _afterDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterDonate‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä

        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: false,‚êä
                afterInitialize: true,‚êä

                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä

## access control (ownable) AntiSandwichHook

## pausable AntiSandwichHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {AntiSandwichHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/AntiSandwichHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Override \`_afterSwapHandler\` to determine how accumulated penalty fees are handled‚êä
    // i.e. distributing the fees to well-behaved LPs, improving swap pricing, etc‚êä
    contract MyHook is AntiSandwichHook, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterSwapHandler(PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, uint256 targetUnspecifiedAmount, uint256 feeAmount)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated penalty fees from sandwich attacks are handled after swaps‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä
                afterInitialize: true,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: true,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä

## shares erc6909 AntiSandwichHook

## basic LiquidityPenaltyHook

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä

    ‚êä

    ‚êä
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty‚êä
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity‚êä
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, ERC20 {‚êä

    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";‚êä
    import {CurrencySettler} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/utils/CurrencySettler.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty‚êä
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity‚êä
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, ERC20 {‚êä
        using CurrencySettler for Currency;‚êä
    ‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4, int128)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä
                afterInitialize: true,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: true,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä
    `

            internal‚êä

## pausable LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty‚êä
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity‚êä
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4, int128)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä
                afterInitialize: true,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: true,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä

    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    contract MyHook is LimitOrderHook, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä

        }‚êä

            public‚êä

            whenNotPaused‚êä
        {‚êä
            super.placeOrder(key, tick, zeroForOne, liquidity);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function cancelOrder(PoolKey calldata key, int24 tickLower, bool zeroForOne, address to)‚êä

## basic ReHypothecationHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {ReHypothecationHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/ReHypothecationHook.sol";‚êä

    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the rehypothecation logic‚êä

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä

    ‚êä
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä

    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {ReHypothecationHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/ReHypothecationHook.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the rehypothecation logic‚êä
    // i.e. keeping the liquidity in a yield-bearing ERC-4626 Vault while still being available for swaps, etc‚êä
    contract MyHook is ReHypothecationHook, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getCurrencyYieldSource(Currency currency)‚êä
            public‚êä
            view‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (address)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the yield source address is computed for a given currency‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _depositToYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is deposited to it's corresponding yield source‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _withdrawFromYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is withdrawn from it's corresponding yield source‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _getAmountInYieldSource(Currency currency)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            view‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (uint256)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement how the hook's balance of a given currency in it's corresponding yield source is obtained‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä

        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä

            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä

        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function addReHypothecatedLiquidity(uint256 shares)‚êä
            public‚êä
            payable‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (BalanceDelta)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super.addReHypothecatedLiquidity(shares);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function removeReHypothecatedLiquidity(uint256 shares)‚êä

        }‚êä

            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä

        }‚êä

                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä

    ‚êä

    ‚êä
    // TODO: Determine the max absolute tick delta for the truncated oracle‚êä

    contract MyHook is BaseOracleHook, ERC20 {‚êä

## access control (managed) BaseOracleHook

## pausable BaseOracleHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseOracleHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/oracles/panoptic/BaseOracleHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Determine the max absolute tick delta for the truncated oracle‚êä
    // i.e. \`488\` to limit tick changes per observation to an equivalent of 5% abrupt price changes‚êä
    // i.e. \`887272\` to disable truncation and allow full tick range observations‚êä
    contract MyHook is BaseOracleHook, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {‚êä
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            BaseOracleHook(887272)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4, int128)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function getHookPermissions()‚êä
            public‚êä
            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return Hooks.Permissions({‚êä
                beforeInitialize: true,‚êä
                afterInitialize: true,‚êä
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidity: true,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,‚êä
                beforeSwap: true,‚êä
                afterSwap: true,‚êä
                beforeDonate: true,‚êä
                afterDonate: false,‚êä
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,‚êä
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true‚êä
            });‚êä
        }‚êä
    }‚êä

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT‚êä
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.6.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.1‚êä
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;‚êä
    ‚êä
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";‚êä
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";‚êä
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";‚êä
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";‚êä
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";‚êä
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    import {OracleHookWithV3Adapters} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/oracles/panoptic/OracleHookWithV3Adapters.sol";‚êä
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";‚êä
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";‚êä
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";‚êä
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";‚êä
    ‚êä
    // TODO: Determine the max absolute tick delta for the truncated oracle‚êä
    // i.e. \`488\` to limit tick changes per observation to an equivalent of 5% abrupt price changes‚êä
    // i.e. \`887272\` to disable truncation and allow full tick range observations‚êä

        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)‚êä
            BaseHook(_poolManager)‚êä
            OracleHookWithV3Adapters(887272)‚êä
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")‚êä
            Ownable(initialOwner)‚êä
        {}‚êä
    ‚êä
        function pause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _pause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {‚êä
            _unpause();‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            whenNotPaused‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä
            internal‚êä
            override‚êä
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)‚êä
        {‚êä
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity‚êä
        }‚êä
    ‚êä
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)‚êä

        }‚êä

        function getHookPermissions()‚êä

            pure‚êä
            override‚êä
